3485         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3486           classfile_parse_error(
3487             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in Record component in class file %s",
3488             attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3489         }
3490         generic_sig_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_0);
3491 
3492       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3493         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3494           classfile_parse_error(
3495             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3496         }
3497         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3498         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3499 
3500         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3501         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3502         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3503 
3504       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3505         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3506           classfile_parse_error(
3507             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3508         }
3509         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3510         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3511           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3512           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3513           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3514         }
3515         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3516 
3517       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3518         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3519           classfile_parse_error(
3520             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3521         }
3522         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3523         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3524 
3525         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3526         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3527         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3528 
3529       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3530         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3531           classfile_parse_error(
3532             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3533         }
3534         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3535         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3536           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3537           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3538           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3539         }
3540         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3541 
3542       } else {
3543         // Skip unknown attributes
3544         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3545       }
3546       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3547     } // End of attributes For loop
3548 
3549     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3550                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3551                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3552                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3553                                                         CHECK_0);
3554     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3555                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3556                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3557                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3558                                                              CHECK_0);
3559 
3560     RecordComponent* record_component =
3561       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3562                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3563                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3564     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3565   }  // End of component processing loop
3566 
3567   // Restore buffer's current position.
3568   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3569   return calculate_attr_size;
3570 }
3571 
3572 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3573   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3574 }
3575 
3576 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3577   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3578 
3579   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3580   check_property(
3581     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3582     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3583     signature_index, CHECK);
3584   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3585 }
3586 
3587 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3588                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3589                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3590                                                                   TRAPS) {
3591   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3592   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3593 
3594   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3595 
3596   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3597                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3598                      attribute_byte_length,
3599                      CHECK);
3600 
3601   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3602 
3603   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3604 
3605   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3606                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3607                      CHECK);
3608 
3609 
3610   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3611   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3612   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3613   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3614   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3615 
3616   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3617   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3618   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3619 
3620   Array<u2>* const operands =
3621     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3622 
3623   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3624   // pool if there is an error.
3625   cp->set_operands(operands);
3626 
3627   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3628   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3629 
3630   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3631     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3632     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3633 
3634     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3635     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3636     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3637     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3638     check_property(
3639       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3640       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3641       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3642       bootstrap_method_index,
3643       CHECK);
3644 
3645     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3646       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3647       CHECK);
3648 
3649     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3650     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3651 
3652     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3653     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3654       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3655       check_property(
3656         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3657         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3658         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3659         argument_index,
3660         CHECK);
3661       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3662     }
3663   }
3664   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3665                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3666                      CHECK);
3667 }
3668 
3669 bool ClassFileParser::supports_sealed_types() {
3670   // temporarily disable the sealed type preview feature check
3671   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
3672 }
3673 
3674 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3675   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3676          _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3677          Arguments::enable_preview();
3678 }
3679 
3680 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3681                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3682                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3683                                                  TRAPS) {
3684   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3685   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3686   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3687 
3688   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3689   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3690   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3691   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3692   // Set _permitted_subclasses attribute to default sentinel
3693   _permitted_subclasses = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3694   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3695   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3696   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3697   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3698   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3699   bool parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute = false;
3700   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3701   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3702   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3703   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3704   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3705   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3706   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3707   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3708   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3709   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3710   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3711   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3712   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3713   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3714   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3715   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3716   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3717   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3718   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3719   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3720   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3721   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3722   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3723   const u1* permitted_subclasses_attribute_start = NULL;
3724   u4  permitted_subclasses_attribute_length = 0;
3725 
3726   // Iterate over attributes
3727   while (attributes_count--) {
3728     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3729     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3730     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3731     check_property(
3732       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3733       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3734       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3735     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3736     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3737       // Check for SourceFile tag
3738       if (_need_verify) {
3739         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3740       }
3741       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3742         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3743       } else {
3744         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3745       }
3746       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3747     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3748       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3749       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3750           classfile_parse_error(
3751             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3752       }
3753       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3754       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3755     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3756       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3757       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3758         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3759       } else {
3760         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3761       }
3762       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3763       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3764       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3765     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3766       // Check for Synthetic tag
3767       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3768       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3769         classfile_parse_error(
3770           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3771           attribute_length, CHECK);
3772       }
3773       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3774     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3775       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3776       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3777         classfile_parse_error(
3778           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3779           attribute_length, CHECK);
3780       }
3781     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3782       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3783         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3784           classfile_parse_error(
3785             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3786         }
3787         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3788           classfile_parse_error(
3789             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3790             attribute_length, CHECK);
3791         }
3792         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3793       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3794         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3795           classfile_parse_error(
3796             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3797         }
3798         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3799         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3800         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3801         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3802         parse_annotations(cp,
3803                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3804                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3805                           parsed_annotations,
3806                           _loader_data,
3807                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
3808                           CHECK);
3809         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3810       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3811         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3812           classfile_parse_error(
3813             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3814         }
3815         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3816         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3817           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3818           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3819           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3820         }
3821         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3822       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3823         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3824           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3825         } else {
3826           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3827         }
3828         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3829           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3830           attribute_length, CHECK);
3831         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3832         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3833         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3834         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3835           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3836         }
3837         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3838         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3839           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3840         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3841             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3842              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3843           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3844         }
3845       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3846                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3847         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3848           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3849         }
3850         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3851         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3852       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3853         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3854           classfile_parse_error(
3855             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3856         }
3857         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3858         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3859         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3860         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3861         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3862       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3863         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3864           classfile_parse_error(
3865             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3866         } else {
3867           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3868         }
3869         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3870           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3871           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3872           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3873         }
3874         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3875       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3876         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3877           // Check for NestMembers tag
3878           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3879             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3880           } else {
3881             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3882           }
3883           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3884             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3885           }
3886           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3887           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3888           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3889         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3890           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3891             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3892           } else {
3893             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3894           }
3895           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3896             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3897           }
3898           if (_need_verify) {
3899             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3900           }
3901           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3902           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3903           check_property(
3904                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3905                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3906                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3907           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3908         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3909           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3910             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3911             // not java.lang.Record.
3912             if (supports_records() &&
3913                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3914               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3915                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3916               }
3917               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3918               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3919                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3920               }
3921               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3922               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3923               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3924             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3925               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3926               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3927               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3928               // exception would have been thrown.
3929               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3930               if (supports_records()) {
3931                 log_info(class, record)(
3932                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3933                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3934               } else {
3935                 log_info(class, record)(
3936                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3937                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3938               }
3939             }
3940             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3941           } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_15_VERSION) {
3942             // Check for PermittedSubclasses tag
3943             if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_permitted_subclasses()) {
3944               if (supports_sealed_types()) {
3945                 if (parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute) {
3946                   classfile_parse_error("Multiple PermittedSubclasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3947                 }
3948                 // Classes marked ACC_FINAL cannot have a PermittedSubclasses attribute.
3949                 if (_access_flags.is_final()) {
3950                   classfile_parse_error("PermittedSubclasses attribute in final class file %s", CHECK);
3951                 }
3952                 parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute = true;
3953                 permitted_subclasses_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3954                 permitted_subclasses_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3955               }
3956               cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3957             } else {
3958               // Unknown attribute
3959               cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3960             }
3961           } else {
3962             // Unknown attribute
3963             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3964           }
3965         } else {
3966           // Unknown attribute
3967           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3968         }
3969       } else {
3970         // Unknown attribute
3971         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3972       }
3973     } else {
3974       // Unknown attribute
3975       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3976     }
3977   }
3978   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3979                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3980                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3981                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3982                                             CHECK);
3983   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3984                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3985                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3986                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3987                                                  CHECK);
3988 
3989   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3990     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3991                             cfs,
3992                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3993                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3994                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3995                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3996                             CHECK);
3997     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3998       guarantee_property(
3999         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
4000         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4001     }
4002   }
4003 
4004   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
4005     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
4006                             cfs,
4007                             nest_members_attribute_start,
4008                             CHECK);
4009     if (_need_verify) {
4010       guarantee_property(
4011         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
4012         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4013     }
4014   }
4015 
4016   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
4017     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
4018                             cfs,
4019                             cp,
4020                             record_attribute_start,
4021                             CHECK);
4022     if (_need_verify) {
4023       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
4024                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
4025                          CHECK);
4026     }
4027   }
4028 
4029   if (parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute) {
4030     const u2 num_subclasses = parse_classfile_permitted_subclasses_attribute(
4031                             cfs,
4032                             permitted_subclasses_attribute_start,
4033                             CHECK);
4034     if (_need_verify) {
4035       guarantee_property(
4036         permitted_subclasses_attribute_length == sizeof(num_subclasses) + sizeof(u2) * num_subclasses,
4037         "Wrong PermittedSubclasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4038     }
4039   }
4040 
4041   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
4042     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
4043                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
4044   }
4045 }
4046 
4047 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
4048   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
4049 
4050   if (_synthetic_flag)
4051     k->set_is_synthetic();
4052   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
4053     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
4054   }
4055   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
4056     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
4057   }
4058   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
4059     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
4060   }
4061 }
4062 
4063 // Create the Annotations object that will
4064 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
4065 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
4066     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
4067         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
4068         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
4069         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
4070       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
4071       return;
4072     }
4073 
4074     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
4075     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
4076     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
4077     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
4078     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4079 
4080     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4081     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4082     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4083 
4084     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4085     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4086     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4087     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4088     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4089     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4090 }
4091 
4092 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4093 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4094                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4095                                             int java_fields_count,
4096                                             TRAPS) {
4097   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4098 
4099   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4100   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4101   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4102   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4103   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4104   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4105   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4106   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4107   this_klass->set_permitted_subclasses(_permitted_subclasses);
4108   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4109   // Delay the setting of _local_interfaces and _transitive_interfaces until after
4110   // initialize_supers() in fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _local_interfaces could
4111   // be shared with _transitive_interfaces and _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4112   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4113   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4114   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4115   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4116 
4117   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4118   clear_class_metadata();
4119 }
4120 
4121 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4122                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4123                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4124                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4125                                                        TRAPS) {
4126   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4127   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4128       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4129     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4130                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4131                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4132                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4133     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4134       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4135         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4136       }
4137     }
4138     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4139       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4140         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4141         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4142       }
4143     }
4144   }
4145   return annotations;
4146 }
4147 
4148 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4149                                                         const int super_class_index,
4150                                                         const bool need_verify,
4151                                                         TRAPS) {
4152   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4153   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4154 
4155   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4156     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4157                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_INLINE),
4158                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4159                    super_class_index,
4160                    CHECK_NULL);
4161   } else {
4162     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4163                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4164                    super_class_index,
4165                    CHECK_NULL);
4166     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4167     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4168     bool is_array = false;
4169     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4170       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4171       if (need_verify)
4172         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4173     } else if (need_verify) {
4174       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4175     }
4176     if (need_verify) {
4177       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4178                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4179     }
4180   }
4181   return super_klass;
4182 }
4183 
4184 #ifndef PRODUCT
4185 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4186                                Array<u2>* fields,
4187                                ConstantPool* cp,
4188                                int instance_size,
4189                                int instance_fields_start,
4190                                int instance_fields_end,
4191                                int static_fields_end) {
4192 
4193   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4194 
4195   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4196   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4197   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4198     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4199       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4200         fs.offset(),
4201         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4202         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4203     }
4204   }
4205   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4206   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4207   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4208   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4209     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4210       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4211         fs.offset(),
4212         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4213         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4214     }
4215   }
4216   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4217   tty->print("\n");
4218 }
4219 #endif
4220 
4221 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4222   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4223   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4224   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4225     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4226   } else {
4227     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4228         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4229     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4230   }
4231 }
4232 
4233 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4234   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4235   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4236 }
4237 
4238 // addition of super oop maps
4239 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4240   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4241          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4242 
4243   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4244   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4245 }
4246 
4247 // collection of oops
4248 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4249   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4250     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4251   }
4252   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4253   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4254     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4255     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4256   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4257     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4258   } else { // Need a new one...
4259     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4260     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4261     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4262     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4263     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4264   }
4265 }
4266 
4267 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4268 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4269   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4270     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4271   }
4272 }
4273 
4274 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4275 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4276   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4277     return;
4278   }
4279   /*
4280    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4281    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4282    * containing refs.
4283    *
4284    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4285    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4286    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4287    */
4288   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4289         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4290   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4291     return;
4292   }
4293 
4294   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4295   ResourceMark rm;
4296   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4297       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4298   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4299   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4300   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4301   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4302   oop_maps_copy++;
4303   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4304     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4305     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4306       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4307     } else {
4308       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4309       new_count++;
4310       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4311       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4312     }
4313     oop_maps_copy++;
4314   }
4315   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4316   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4317 }
4318 
4319 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4320   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4321   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4322     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4323     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4324     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4325     while (map <= last_map) {
4326       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4327                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4328       map++;
4329     }
4330   }
4331 }
4332 
4333 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4334   print_on(st);
4335 }
4336 
4337 void ClassFileParser::throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4338                                                 const char* msg,
4339                                                 const Symbol* name,
4340                                                 const Symbol* sig) const {
4341 
4342   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4343   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4344     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4345         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4346         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4347   }
4348   else {
4349     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4350         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4351         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4352         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4353   }
4354 }
4355 
4356 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4357 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4358                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4359                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4360                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4361                                     TRAPS) {
4362 
4363   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4364 
4365   // Field size and offset computation
4366   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4367                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4368   int next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4369   int first_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4370 
4371   // Fields that are inline types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4372   // - static fields are oops
4373   // - non-static fields are embedded
4374 
4375   // Count the contended fields by type.
4376   //
4377   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4378   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4379   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4380   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4381   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4382     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4383     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4384       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4385       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4386         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4387       }
4388     }
4389   }
4390 
4391 
4392   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4393   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4394   // Inline types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4395   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4396                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]) * heapOopSize);
4397   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4398     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4399   }
4400 
4401   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4402                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4403   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4404                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4405   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4406                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4407 
4408   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4409                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4410 
4411   // First field of inline types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4412   // in-lining of inline types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4413   // inlined fields
4414   int initial_inline_type_padding = 0;
4415   if (is_inline_type()) {
4416     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4417     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4418     initial_inline_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4419   }
4420 
4421   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4422 
4423   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4424 
4425   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4426   if (is_contended_class) {
4427     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4428   }
4429 
4430   // Temporary inline types restrictions
4431   if (is_inline_type()) {
4432     if (is_contended_class) {
4433       throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4434       return;
4435     }
4436   }
4437 
4438   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4439   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4440   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4441   // exempt from that.
4442   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4443   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4444   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4445   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4446   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4447 
4448   int static_inline_type_count = 0;
4449   int nonstatic_inline_type_count = 0;
4450   int* nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NULL;
4451   Klass** nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NULL;
4452   unsigned int inline_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4453   int inline_types_not_inlined = 0;
4454   int not_atomic_inline_types = 0;
4455 
4456   int max_nonstatic_inline_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE] + 1;
4457 
4458   nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4459                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4460   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_inline_type; i++) {
4461     nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4462   }
4463   nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4464                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4465 
4466   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4467     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_INLINE) {
4468       ResourceMark rm;
4469       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4470         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4471       }
4472       static_inline_type_count++;
4473     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_INLINE) {
4474       // Pre-resolve the inline field and check for inline type circularity issues.
4475       ResourceMark rm;
4476       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4477         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4478       }
4479       Klass* klass =
4480         SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_type_field_or_fail(&fs,
4481                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4482                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4483       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4484       if (!klass->access_flags().is_inline_type()) {
4485         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4486       }
4487       InlineKlass* vk = InlineKlass::cast(klass);
4488       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4489       bool too_big_to_allocate_inline = (InlineFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4490                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > InlineFieldMaxFlatSize);
4491       bool too_atomic_to_allocate_inline = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4492       bool too_volatile_to_allocate_inline = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4493       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4494         too_atomic_to_allocate_inline = false;
4495         // too_volatile_to_allocate_inline = false; //FIXME
4496         // volatile fields are currently never inlined, this could change in the future
4497       }
4498       if (!(too_big_to_allocate_inline | too_atomic_to_allocate_inline | too_volatile_to_allocate_inline)) {
4499         nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = fs.index();
4500         nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = klass;
4501         nonstatic_inline_type_count++;
4502 
4503         InlineKlass* vklass = InlineKlass::cast(klass);
4504         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4505           inline_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4506         }
4507         fs.set_inlined(true);
4508         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4509           not_atomic_inline_types++;
4510         }
4511       } else {
4512         inline_types_not_inlined++;
4513         fs.set_inlined(false);
4514       }
4515     }
4516   }
4517 
4518   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account inline types fields not inlined;
4519   nonstatic_oop_count += inline_types_not_inlined;
4520 
4521   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4522   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4523                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4524                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE];
4525 
4526   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4527           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4528   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4529     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4530   const bool has_nonstatic_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4531 
4532   if (is_inline_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4533     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4534     throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4535     return;
4536   }
4537 
4538   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4539   //
4540   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4541   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4542   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4543   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4544   // distinct regions.
4545   //
4546   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4547   int max_oop_map_count =
4548       super_oop_map_count +
4549       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4550       inline_type_oop_map_count +
4551       inline_types_not_inlined;
4552 
4553   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4554   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4555     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4556                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4557   }
4558 
4559   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4560 
4561   bool compact_fields  = true;
4562   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4563 
4564   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4565   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4566 
4567   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4568   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4569     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4570     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4571     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4572                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4573   } else {
4574     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4575     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4576   }
4577 
4578   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4579   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4580   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4581   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4582   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4583   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4584   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4585   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4586 
4587   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4588   // long/double alignment.
4589   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4590     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4591     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4592     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4593       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4594       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4595       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4596       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4597       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4598         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4599         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4600         length -= BytesPerInt;
4601         offset += BytesPerInt;
4602       }
4603       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4604       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4605         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4606         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4607         length -= BytesPerShort;
4608         offset += BytesPerShort;
4609       }
4610       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4611       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4612         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4613         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4614         length -= 1;
4615       }
4616       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4617       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4618       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4619           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4620         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4621         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4622         length -= heapOopSize;
4623         offset += heapOopSize;
4624       }
4625     }
4626   }
4627 
4628   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4629                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4630   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4631                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4632   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4633                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4634   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4635                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4636 
4637   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4638   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4639     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4640     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4641       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4642     }
4643     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4644   }
4645 
4646   // Aligning embedded inline types
4647   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded inline types always put them at the
4648   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4649   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4650   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each inline type starting on a
4651   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4652   // align inline types according to their most constrained internal type.
4653   next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4654   int next_inline_type_index = 0;
4655 
4656   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4657   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4658   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4659   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4660 
4661     // skip already laid out fields
4662     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4663 
4664     // contended instance fields are handled below
4665     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4666 
4667     int real_offset = 0;
4668     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4669 
4670     // pack the rest of the fields
4671     switch (atype) {
4672       // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4673       case STATIC_INLINE:   // Fallthrough
4674       case STATIC_OOP:
4675         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4676         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4677         break;
4678       case STATIC_BYTE:
4679         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4680         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4681         break;
4682       case STATIC_SHORT:
4683         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4684         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4685         break;
4686       case STATIC_WORD:
4687         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4688         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4689         break;
4690       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4691         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4692         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4693         break;
4694       case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4695         if (fs.is_inlined()) {
4696           Klass* klass = nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[next_inline_type_index];
4697           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4698           assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(),"Must be an inline type");
4699           InlineKlass* vklass = InlineKlass::cast(klass);
4700           real_offset = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4701           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4702           // aligning next inline type on a 64 bits boundary
4703           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset, BytesPerLong);
4704           next_inline_type_index += 1;
4705 
4706           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4707             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4708             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4709             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4710             while (map < last_map) {
4711               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4712               map++;
4713             }
4714           }
4715           break;
4716         } else {
4717           // Fall through
4718         }
4719       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4720         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4721           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4722           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4723           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4724         } else {
4725           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4726           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4727         }
4728         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4729         break;
4730       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4731         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4732           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4733           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4734           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4735         } else {
4736           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4737           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4738         }
4739         break;
4740       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4741         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4742           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4743           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4744           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4745         } else {
4746           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4747           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4748         }
4749         break;
4750       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4751         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4752           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4753           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4754           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4755         } else {
4756           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4757           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4758         }
4759         break;
4760       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4761         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4762         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4763         break;
4764       default:
4765         ShouldNotReachHere();
4766     }
4767     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4768   }
4769 
4770 
4771   // Handle the contended cases.
4772   //
4773   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4774   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4775   // the fields with full-width padding.
4776   //
4777   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4778   // for each field.
4779   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4780 
4781     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4782     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4783 
4784     // collect all contended groups
4785     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4786     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4787       // skip already laid out fields
4788       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4789 
4790       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4791         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4792       }
4793     }
4794 
4795     int current_group = -1;
4796     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4797 
4798       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4799 
4800         // skip already laid out fields
4801         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4802 
4803         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4804         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4805 
4806         // handle statics below
4807         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4808 
4809         int real_offset = 0;
4810         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4811 
4812         switch (atype) {
4813           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4814             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4815             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4816             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4817             break;
4818 
4819           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4820             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4821             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4822             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4823             break;
4824 
4825           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4826             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4827             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4828             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4829             break;
4830 
4831           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4832             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4833             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4834             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4835             break;
4836 
4837             // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4838           case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4839             throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4840                                       "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4841             return;
4842 
4843           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4844             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4845             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4846             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4847             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4848             break;
4849 
4850           default:
4851             ShouldNotReachHere();
4852         }
4853 
4854         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4855           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4856           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4857           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4858           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4859           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4860         }
4861 
4862         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4863       } // for
4864 
4865       // Start laying out the next group.
4866       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4867       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4868       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4869       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4870       if (current_group != 0) {
4871         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4872       }
4873     }
4874 
4875     // handle static fields
4876   }
4877 
4878   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4879   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4880   // and/or adjacent object.
4881   if (is_contended_class) {
4882     assert(!is_inline_type(), "@Contended not supported for inline types yet");
4883     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4884   }
4885 
4886   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4887   if (nonstatic_inline_type_count != 0) {
4888     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4889   } else {
4890     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4891   }
4892 
4893   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4894   if (is_inline_type()) {
4895     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4896       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4897     }
4898   }
4899   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4900   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4901   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4902 
4903   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4904                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4905   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4906                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4907 
4908   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4909 
4910   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4911          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4912          + initial_inline_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4913 
4914 
4915   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4916   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4917   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4918   // assert without actually having the fields.
4919   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4920          is_contended_class ||
4921          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4922 
4923   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4924   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4925 
4926 #ifndef PRODUCT
4927   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_inline_type()) ||
4928       (PrintInlineLayout && (is_inline_type() || has_nonstatic_inline_fields))) {
4929     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4930           _fields,
4931           cp,
4932           instance_size,
4933           nonstatic_fields_start,
4934           nonstatic_fields_end,
4935           static_fields_end);
4936     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4937     tty->print("\n");
4938     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4939     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4940     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4941     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4942     tty->print_cr("---");
4943   }
4944 
4945 #endif
4946   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4947   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4948   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4949   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4950   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4951   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4952   info->_has_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4953 
4954   // An inline type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4955   // that field is simple enough.
4956   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_inline_type() &&
4957                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4958                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4959                                 (not_atomic_inline_types == 0) &&
4960                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4961   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4962   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4963   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4964   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4965   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4966 }
4967 
4968 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4969   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4970 
4971   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4972 
4973   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4974   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4975   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4976     if (_has_finalizer ||
4977         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4978       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4979     }
4980   }
4981 
4982 #ifdef ASSERT
4983   bool f = false;
4984   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4985                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4986   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4987       f = true;
4988   }
4989 
4990   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4991   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4992   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4993   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4994     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4995   }
4996 #endif
4997 
4998   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4999   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
5000     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
5001       if (ik->is_inline_klass()) {
5002         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
5003         throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
5004         return;
5005       }
5006       ik->set_is_cloneable();
5007     }
5008   }
5009 
5010   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
5011   if (super == NULL) {
5012     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
5013     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
5014   } else {
5015     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
5016         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
5017       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
5018     }
5019 #ifdef ASSERT
5020     bool v = false;
5021     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
5022       const Method* const constructor =
5023         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
5024                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
5025       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
5026         v = true;
5027       }
5028     }
5029     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
5030 #endif
5031   }
5032 
5033   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
5034   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
5035   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
5036   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
5037       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
5038       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
5039       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
5040     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
5041     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
5042     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
5043   }
5044 }
5045 
5046 bool ClassFileParser::supports_inline_types() const {
5047   // Inline types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
5048   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
5049 }
5050 
5051 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
5052 
5053 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
5054                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
5055   // iterate over new interfaces
5056   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
5057     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
5058     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
5059     // add new interface
5060     result->append_if_missing(e);
5061   }
5062 }
5063 
5064 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
5065                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
5066                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
5067                                                             TRAPS) {
5068   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5069   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5070 
5071   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5072   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5073   int super_size = 0;
5074   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5075   if (super != NULL) {
5076     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5077     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5078   }
5079   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5080   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5081   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5082     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5083     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5084   }
5085   // Finally add local interfaces
5086   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5087   // Construct array
5088   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5089     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5090     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5091   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5092     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5093     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5094     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5095 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5096 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5097 //    return local_ifs;
5098   } else {
5099     ResourceMark rm;
5100     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5101 
5102     // Copy down from superclass
5103     if (super != NULL) {
5104       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5105     }
5106 
5107     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5108     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5109       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5110       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5111     }
5112     // Finally add local interfaces
5113     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5114 
5115     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5116     const int length = result->length();
5117     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5118
