5119     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5120       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5121     }
5122 
5123     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5124       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5125     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5126       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5127       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5128       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5129     }
5130     return new_result;
5131   }
5132 }
5133 
5134 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5135   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5136   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5137 
5138   if (super != NULL) {
5139     const InstanceKlass* super_ik = InstanceKlass::cast(super);
5140 
5141     if (super->is_final()) {
5142       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5143       Exceptions::fthrow(
5144         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5145         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5146         "class %s cannot inherit from final class %s",
5147         this_klass->external_name(),
5148         super_ik->external_name());
5149       return;
5150     }
5151 
5152     if (super_ik->is_sealed() && !super_ik->has_as_permitted_subclass(this_klass)) {
5153       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5154       Exceptions::fthrow(
5155         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5156         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
5157         "class %s cannot inherit from sealed class %s",
5158         this_klass->external_name(),
5159         super_ik->external_name());
5160       return;
5161     }
5162 
5163     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5164     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5165     // special reflection class loader
5166     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5167       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5168       if (super_package != NULL &&
5169           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5170           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5171         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5172         Exceptions::fthrow(
5173           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5174           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5175           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5176           this_klass->external_name(),
5177           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5178           super->external_name());
5179         return;
5180       }
5181     }
5182 
5183     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5184       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5185     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5186       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5187       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5188                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5189                                                       vca_result);
5190       if (msg == NULL) {
5191         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5192         Exceptions::fthrow(
5193           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5194           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5195           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5196           this_klass->external_name(),
5197           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5198           super->external_name(),
5199           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5200           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5201           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5202       } else {
5203         // Add additional message content.
5204         Exceptions::fthrow(
5205           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5206           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5207           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5208           msg);
5209       }
5210     }
5211   }
5212 }
5213 
5214 
5215 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5216   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5217   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5218   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5219   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5220     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5221     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5222 
5223     if (k->is_sealed() && !k->has_as_permitted_subclass(this_klass)) {
5224       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5225       Exceptions::fthrow(
5226         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5227         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
5228         "class %s cannot %s sealed interface %s",
5229         this_klass->external_name(),
5230         this_klass->is_interface() ? "extend" : "implement",
5231         k->external_name());
5232       return;
5233     }
5234 
5235     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5236       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5237     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5238       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5239       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5240                                                       k,
5241                                                       vca_result);
5242       if (msg == NULL) {
5243         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5244         Exceptions::fthrow(
5245           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5246           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5247           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5248           this_klass->external_name(),
5249           k->external_name(),
5250           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5251           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5252           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5253       } else {
5254         // Add additional message content.
5255         Exceptions::fthrow(
5256           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5257           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5258           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5259           msg);
5260       }
5261     }
5262   }
5263 }
5264 
5265 
5266 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5267   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5268   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5269   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5270 
5271   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5272   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5273     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5274 
5275     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5276     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5277         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5278 
5279       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5280       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5281       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5282       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5283       while (k != NULL) {
5284         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5285         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5286           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5287           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5288           if (super_m == NULL) {
5289             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5290           }
5291 
5292           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5293               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5294             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5295             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5296                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5297                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5298                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5299                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5300             if (can_access) {
5301               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5302               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5303               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5304                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5305                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5306                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5307                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5308                                  name->as_C_string(),
5309                                  signature->as_C_string()
5310                                  );
5311               return;
5312             }
5313           }
5314 
5315           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5316           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5317           continue;
5318         }
5319 
5320         k = k->super();
5321       }
5322     }
5323   }
5324 }
5325 
5326 
5327 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5328 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5329   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5330   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5331   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5332   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5333 
5334   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5335     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5336     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5337     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5338       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5339       Exceptions::fthrow(
5340         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5341         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5342         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5343         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5344         this_klass->external_name()
5345       );
5346       return;
5347     }
5348   }
5349 }
5350 
5351 // utility methods for format checking
5352 
5353 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5354   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5355   const bool is_inline_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_INLINE) != 0;
5356   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5357   assert(supports_inline_types() || !is_inline_type, "JVM_ACC_INLINE should not be set");
5358   if (is_module) {
5359     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5360     Exceptions::fthrow(
5361       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5362       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5363       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5364       _class_name->as_C_string());
5365     return;
5366   }
5367 
5368   if (is_inline_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5369     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5370     Exceptions::fthrow(
5371       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5372       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5373       "Class modifier ACC_INLINE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5374       _class_name->as_C_string()
5375     );
5376   }
5377 
5378   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5379 
5380   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5381   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5382   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5383   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5384   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5385   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5386   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5387   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5388 
5389   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5390       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5391       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5392       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5393       (is_inline_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5394     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5395     const char* class_note = "";
5396     if (is_inline_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5397     Exceptions::fthrow(
5398       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5399       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5400       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5401       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5402     );
5403     return;
5404   }
5405 }
5406 
5407 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5408   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5409   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5410   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5411 
5412   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5413           (is_public && is_private) ||
5414           (is_protected && is_private));
5415 }
5416 
5417 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5418 //
5419 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5420 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5421 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5422 //
5423 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5424   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5425   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5426   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5427     Exceptions::fthrow(
5428       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5429       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5430       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5431       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5432     return;
5433   }
5434 
5435   if (major > max_version) {
5436     Exceptions::fthrow(
5437       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5438       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5439       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5440       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5441       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5442     return;
5443   }
5444 
5445   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5446     return;
5447   }
5448 
5449   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5450     if (major != max_version) {
5451       Exceptions::fthrow(
5452         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5453         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5454         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5455         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5456         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5457       return;
5458     }
5459 
5460     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5461       Exceptions::fthrow(
5462         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5463         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5464         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5465         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5466       return;
5467     }
5468 
5469   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5470     Exceptions::fthrow(
5471         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5472         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5473         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5474         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5475   }
5476 }
5477 
5478 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5479                                                    bool is_interface,
5480                                                    bool is_inline_type,
5481                                                    TRAPS) const {
5482   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5483 
5484   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5485   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5486   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5487   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5488   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5489   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5490   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5491   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5492   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5493 
5494   bool is_illegal = false;
5495 
5496   if (is_interface) {
5497     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5498         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5499         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5500       is_illegal = true;
5501     }
5502   } else { // not interface
5503     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5504       is_illegal = true;
5505     } else {
5506       if (is_inline_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5507         is_illegal = true;
5508       }
5509     }
5510   }
5511 
5512   if (is_illegal) {
5513     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5514     Exceptions::fthrow(
5515       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5516       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5517       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5518       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5519     return;
5520   }
5521 }
5522 
5523 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5524                                                     bool is_interface,
5525                                                     bool is_inline_type,
5526                                                     const Symbol* name,
5527                                                     TRAPS) const {
5528   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5529 
5530   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5531   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5532   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5533   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5534   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5535   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5536   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5537   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5538   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5539   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5540   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5541   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5542   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5543 
5544   bool is_illegal = false;
5545 
5546   const char* class_note = "";
5547 
5548   if (is_interface) {
5549     if (major_gte_8) {
5550       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5551       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5552       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5553       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5554       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5555           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5556           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5557           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5558           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5559           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5560           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5561           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5562           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5563         is_illegal = true;
5564       }
5565     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5566       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5567       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5568           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5569         is_illegal = true;
5570       }
5571     } else {
5572       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5573       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5574         is_illegal = true;
5575       }
5576     }
5577   } else { // not interface
5578     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5579       is_illegal = true;
5580     } else {
5581       if (is_initializer) {
5582         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5583             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5584           is_illegal = true;
5585         }
5586         if (!is_static && !is_inline_type) {
5587           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5588         } else if (is_static && is_inline_type) {
5589           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5590         } else {
5591           // but no other combinations are allowed
5592           is_illegal = true;
5593           class_note = (is_inline_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5594         }
5595       } else { // not initializer
5596         if (is_inline_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5597           is_illegal = true;
5598           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5599         } else {
5600           if (is_abstract) {
5601             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5602                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5603               is_illegal = true;
5604             }
5605           }
5606         }
5607       }
5608     }
5609   }
5610 
5611   if (is_illegal) {
5612     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5613     Exceptions::fthrow(
5614       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5615       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5616       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5617       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5618     return;
5619   }
5620 }
5621 
5622 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5623                                         int length,
5624                                         TRAPS) const {
5625   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5626   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5627     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5628   }
5629 }
5630 
5631 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5632 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5633 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5634 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5635 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5636 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5637 //
5638 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5639 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5640 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5641                                               unsigned int length,
5642                                               int type) {
5643   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5644   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5645     switch(*p) {
5646       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5647       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5648       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5649         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5650         return false;
5651       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5652         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5653         // unqualified name must not be empty
5654         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5655           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5656               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5657             return false;
5658           }
5659         } else {
5660           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5661         }
5662         break;
5663       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5664       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5665         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5666         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5667           return false;
5668         }
5669     }
5670   }
5671   return true;
5672 }
5673 
5674 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5675 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5676 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5677 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5678 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5679 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5680 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5681 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5682                                         bool slash_ok,
5683                                         unsigned int length) {
5684   const char* p;
5685   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5686   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5687 
5688   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5689     const char* old_p = p;
5690     jchar ch = *p;
5691     if (ch < 128) {
5692       p++;
5693       // quick check for ascii
5694       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5695         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5696         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5697         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5698         last_is_slash = false;
5699         continue;
5700       }
5701       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5702         if (last_is_slash) {
5703           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5704         }
5705         last_is_slash = true;
5706         continue;
5707       }
5708     }
5709     else {
5710       jint unicode_ch;
5711       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5712       p = tmp_p;
5713       last_is_slash = false;
5714       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5715       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5716       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5717       // return value
5718       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5719       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5720       JavaCallArguments args;
5721       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5722 
5723       if (not_first_ch) {
5724         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5725         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5726           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5727           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5728           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5729           &args,
5730           THREAD);
5731       } else {
5732         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5733         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5734           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5735           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5736           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5737           &args,
5738           THREAD);
5739       }
5740       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5741         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5742         return NULL;
5743       }
5744       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5745         continue;
5746       }
5747     }
5748     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5749   }
5750   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5751 }
5752 
5753 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5754 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5755 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5756 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5757 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5758 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5759                                                        bool void_ok,
5760                                                        unsigned int length,
5761                                                        TRAPS) const {
5762   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5763   while (length > 0) {
5764     switch (signature[0]) {
5765     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5766     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5767     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5768     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5769     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5770     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5771     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5772     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5773     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5774       return signature + 1;
5775     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INLINE_TYPE:
5776       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5777       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5778       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5779       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5780       //                                    CHECK_0);
5781       // }
5782       // fall through
5783     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5784     {
5785       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5786         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5787         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5788 
5789         // The next character better be a semicolon
5790         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5791           return p + 1;
5792         }
5793       }
5794       else {
5795         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5796         signature++;
5797         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5798         // Format check signature
5799         if (c != NULL) {
5800           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5801           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5802           if (!legal) {
5803             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5804                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5805                                   CHECK_NULL);
5806             return NULL;
5807           }
5808           return signature + newlen + 1;
5809         }
5810       }
5811       return NULL;
5812     }
5813     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5814       array_dim++;
5815       if (array_dim > 255) {
5816         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5817         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5818       }
5819       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5820       signature++;
5821       length--;
5822       void_ok = false;
5823       break;
5824     default:
5825       return NULL;
5826     }
5827   }
5828   return NULL;
5829 }
5830 
5831 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5832 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5833   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5834 
5835   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5836   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5837   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5838   bool legal = false;
5839 
5840   if (length > 0) {
5841     const char* p;
5842     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5843       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5844       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5845     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5846       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5847         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5848         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5849       }
5850     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5851       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5852       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5853     } else {
5854       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5855       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5856       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5857       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5858       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5859     }
5860   }
5861   if (!legal) {
5862     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5863     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5864     Exceptions::fthrow(
5865       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5866       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5867       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5868       _class_name->as_C_string()
5869     );
5870     return;
5871   }
5872 }
5873 
5874 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5875 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5876   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5877 
5878   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5879   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5880   bool legal = false;
5881 
5882   if (length > 0) {
5883     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5884       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5885         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5886         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5887       }
5888     } else {
5889       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5890       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5891     }
5892   }
5893 
5894   if (!legal) {
5895     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5896     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5897     Exceptions::fthrow(
5898       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5899       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5900       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5901       _class_name->as_C_string()
5902     );
5903     return;
5904   }
5905 }
5906 
5907 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5908 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5909   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5910 
5911   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5912   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5913   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5914   bool legal = false;
5915 
5916   if (length > 0) {
5917     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5918       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5919         legal = true;
5920       }
5921     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5922       const char* p;
5923       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5924       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5925     } else {
5926       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5927       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5928     }
5929   }
5930 
5931   if (!legal) {
5932     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5933     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5934     Exceptions::fthrow(
5935       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5936       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5937       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5938       _class_name->as_C_string()
5939     );
5940     return;
5941   }
5942 }
5943 
5944 
5945 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5946 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5947                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5948                                                    TRAPS) const {
5949   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5950 
5951   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5952   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5953   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5954 
5955   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5956     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5957   }
5958 }
5959 
5960 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5961 // Returns number of parameters
5962 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5963                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5964                                                    TRAPS) const {
5965   if (!_need_verify) {
5966     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5967     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5968     return -2;
5969   }
5970 
5971   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5972   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5973       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5974       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5975     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5976     return 0;
5977   }
5978 
5979   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5980   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5981   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5982   const char* nextp;
5983 
5984   // The first character must be a '('
5985   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5986     length--;
5987     // Skip over legal field signatures
5988     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5989     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5990       args_size++;
5991       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5992         args_size++;
5993       }
5994       length -= nextp - p;
5995       p = nextp;
5996       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5997     }
5998     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5999     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
6000       length--;
6001       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
6002         // All constructor methods must return void
6003         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
6004           return args_size;
6005         }
6006         // All static init methods must return the current class
6007         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
6008             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6009           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
6010           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
6011             // The actual class will be checked against current class
6012             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
6013             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
6014             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
6015             return args_size;
6016           }
6017         }
6018         // The distinction between static factory methods and
6019         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
6020         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
6021         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
6022       } else {
6023         // Now we better just have a return value
6024         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
6025         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
6026           return args_size;
6027         }
6028       }
6029     }
6030   }
6031   // Report error
6032   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
6033   return 0;
6034 }
6035 
6036 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
6037   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6038   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
6039 }
