6041 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
6042   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6043   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
6044 }
6045 
6046 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
6047   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6048   return _field_info->_instance_size;
6049 }
6050 
6051 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
6052                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
6053   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6054   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6055 
6056   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
6057   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
6058   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
6059   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
6060   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
6061 
6062   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
6063     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6064       Method* method = methods->at(j);
6065       method->init_intrinsic_id();
6066 
6067       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6068         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
6069         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
6070         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
6071             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
6072               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6073               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
6074               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6075               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6076             );
6077           tty->cr();
6078           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6079         }
6080         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
6081         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
6082         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
6083           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
6084             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
6085               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
6086               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6087               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6088             );
6089           tty->cr();
6090           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6091         }
6092       }
6093     } // end for
6094 
6095 #ifdef ASSERT
6096     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6097       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
6098       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
6099       // but class C does not declare m.
6100       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
6101       // only in debug builds.
6102 
6103       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6104         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6105           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6106           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6107           // is defined for it.
6108           continue;
6109         }
6110 
6111         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6112           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6113           // name, flags, signature.
6114           bool match = false;
6115           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6116             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6117             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6118               match = true;
6119               break;
6120             }
6121           }
6122 
6123           if (!match) {
6124             char buf[1000];
6125             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6126                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6127                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6128                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6129                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6130                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6131             );
6132             tty->cr();
6133             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6134           }
6135         }
6136       } // end for
6137     } // CheckIntrinsics
6138 #endif // ASSERT
6139   }
6140 }
6141 
6142 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook,
6143                                                       const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6144                                                       TRAPS) {
6145   if (_klass != NULL) {
6146     return _klass;
6147   }
6148 
6149   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6150     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6151 
6152   if (is_hidden()) {
6153     mangle_hidden_class_name(ik);
6154   }
6155 
6156   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, cl_inst_info, CHECK_NULL);
6157 
6158   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6159 
6160 
6161   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6162     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6163   }
6164 
6165   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6166   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6167     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6168     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6169     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6170       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6171       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6172     } else {
6173       ResourceMark rm;
6174       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6175                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6176     }
6177   }
6178 
6179   if (ik->is_inline_klass()) {
6180     InlineKlass* vk = InlineKlass::cast(ik);
6181     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6182     vk->set_default_value(val);
6183   }
6184 
6185   return ik;
6186 }
6187 
6188 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6189 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6190 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6191 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6192 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6193 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6194 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6195 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6196   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6197     return true;
6198   }
6199   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6200     return false;
6201   }
6202   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6203     return true;
6204   } else {
6205     // Look at each method
6206     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6207       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6208       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6209         return true;
6210 
6211       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6212         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6213             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6214           return true;
6215         }
6216       }
6217     }
6218   }
6219   return false;
6220 }
6221 
6222 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik,
6223                                           bool changed_by_loadhook,
6224                                           const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6225                                           TRAPS) {
6226   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6227 
6228   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6229   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6230   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6231 
6232   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6233   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6234   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6235 
6236   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6237 
6238   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6239 
6240   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6241   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6242   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6243          "sanity");
6244 
6245   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6246   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6247 
6248   // Fill in information already parsed
6249   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6250 
6251   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6252   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6253   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6254   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_inline_klass()) {
6255     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6256   }
6257   if (_is_empty_inline_type) {
6258     ik->set_is_empty_inline_type();
6259   }
6260 
6261   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6262     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6263   }
6264 
6265   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6266     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6267   }
6268 
6269   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6270   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]);
6271 
6272   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6273   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6274   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6275 
6276   // can only set dynamic nest-host after static nest information is set
6277   if (cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host() != NULL) {
6278     ik->set_nest_host(cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host(), THREAD);
6279   }
6280 
6281   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6282   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6283   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6284   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6285   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6286   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6287   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6288   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6289   assert(NULL == _permitted_subclasses, "invariant");
6290 
6291   if (_has_final_method) {
6292     ik->set_has_final_method();
6293   }
6294 
6295   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6296   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6297   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6298   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6299   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6300   // has to be changed accordingly.
6301   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6302 
6303   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6304 
6305   if (_is_hidden || is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6306     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6307     // hidden or anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own
6308     // methods or fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6309     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is hidden or anonymous (it's
6310     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6311     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6312     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6313     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6314   }
6315 
6316   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6317   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6318   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6319   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6320   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6321     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6322   }
6323 
6324   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6325     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6326     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6327   }
6328   if (_is_hidden) {
6329     ik->set_is_hidden();
6330   }
6331 
6332   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6333   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6334   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6335   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6336   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6337 
6338   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6339   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6340   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6341 
6342   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6343 
6344   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6345   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6346     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6347   }
6348 
6349   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6350 
6351   // Miranda methods
6352   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6353       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6354       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6355         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6356      ) {
6357        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6358   }
6359 
6360   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6361   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6362   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6363   ik->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
6364   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6365   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6366 
6367   // Initialize itable offset tables
6368   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6369 
6370   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6371   // Do final class setup
6372   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6373   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6374     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6375   }
6376 
6377   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6378       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6379     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6380   }
6381 
6382   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6383   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6384 
6385   // check if this class can access its super class
6386   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6387 
6388   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6389   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6390 
6391   // check if this class overrides any final method
6392   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6393 
6394   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6395   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6396     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6397   }
6398 
6399   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6400   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6401   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6402 
6403   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6404   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6405 
6406   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6407   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6408   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6409                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6410                                  module_handle,
6411                                  _protection_domain,
6412                                  cl_inst_info.class_data(),
6413                                  CHECK);
6414 
6415   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6416 
6417   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6418   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6419   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6420     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6421                                              _all_mirandas,
6422                                              CHECK);
6423   }
6424 
6425   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6426   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6427       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6428     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6429       // We won a potential race
6430       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6431     }
6432   }
6433 
6434   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6435   if (ik->is_inline_klass()) nfields++;
6436   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6437     if (ik->field_is_inline_type(i) && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) == 0)) {
6438       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6439       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6440       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6441       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6442           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6443           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6444       if (klass != NULL) {
6445         assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
6446         ik->set_inline_type_field_klass(i, klass);
6447       }
6448       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6449     } else
6450       if (is_inline_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6451         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6452       InlineKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6453     }
6454   }
6455 
6456   if (is_inline_type()) {
6457     InlineKlass* vk = InlineKlass::cast(ik);
6458     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6459       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6460       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6461       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6462     } else {
6463       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6464     }
6465     InlineKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6466   }
6467 
6468   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6469 
6470   if (!is_internal()) {
6471     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6472       ResourceMark rm;
6473       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6474       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6475     }
6476 
6477     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6478         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6479         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6480       ResourceMark rm;
6481       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6482                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6483     }
6484 
6485     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6486       ResourceMark rm;
6487       // print out the superclass.
6488       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6489       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6490         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6491                    from,
6492                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6493       }
6494       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6495       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6496       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6497         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6498         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6499           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6500           const char * to = k->external_name();
6501           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6502         }
6503       }
6504     }
6505   }
6506 
6507   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6508 
6509   // If we reach here, all is well.
6510   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6511   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6512   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6513 
6514   // it's official
6515   set_klass(ik);
6516 
6517   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6518     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6519   }
6520 
6521   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6522 }
6523 
6524 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6525   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6526   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6527 
6528   _class_name = new_class_name;
6529   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6530   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6531   // the destructor.
6532   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6533 }
6534 
6535 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6536 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6537 // its _class_name field.
6538 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6539   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6540   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6541          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6542   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6543     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6544 
6545   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6546     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6547     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6548     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6549     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6550     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6551                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6552     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6553 
6554     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6555     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6556 
6557     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6558     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6559     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6560     // when the class is unloaded.
6561     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6562   }
6563 }
6564 
6565 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6566 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6567 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6568 // exception.
6569 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6570   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6571 
6572   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6573                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6574   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6575     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6576   } else {
6577     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6578       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6579       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6580         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6581         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6582     }
6583   }
6584 }
6585 
6586 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6587   bool trusted = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
6588                  loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data();
6589   bool need_verify =
6590     // verifyAll
6591     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6592     // verifyRemote
6593     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6594   return !need_verify;
6595 }
6596 
6597 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6598                                  Symbol* name,
6599                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6600                                  const ClassLoadInfo* cl_info,
6601                                  Publicity pub_level,
6602                                  TRAPS) :
6603   _stream(stream),
6604   _class_name(NULL),
6605   _loader_data(loader_data),
6606   _unsafe_anonymous_host(cl_info->unsafe_anonymous_host()),
6607   _cp_patches(cl_info->cp_patches()),
6608   _is_hidden(cl_info->is_hidden()),
6609   _can_access_vm_annotations(cl_info->can_access_vm_annotations()),
6610   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6611   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6612   _orig_cp_size(0),
6613   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6614   _super_klass(),
6615   _cp(NULL),
6616   _fields(NULL),
6617   _methods(NULL),
6618   _inner_classes(NULL),
6619   _nest_members(NULL),
6620   _nest_host(0),
6621   _permitted_subclasses(NULL),
6622   _record_components(NULL),
6623   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6624   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6625   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6626   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6627   _class_annotations(NULL),
6628   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6629   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6630   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6631   _klass(NULL),
6632   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6633   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6634   _fac(NULL),
6635   _field_info(NULL),
6636   _method_ordering(NULL),
6637   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6638   _vtable_size(0),
6639   _itable_size(0),
6640   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6641   _rt(REF_NONE),
6642   _protection_domain(cl_info->protection_domain()),
6643   _access_flags(),
6644   _pub_level(pub_level),
6645   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6646   _synthetic_flag(false),
6647   _sde_length(false),
6648   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6649   _sourcefile_index(0),
6650   _generic_signature_index(0),
6651   _major_version(0),
6652   _minor_version(0),
6653   _this_class_index(0),
6654   _super_class_index(0),
6655   _itfs_len(0),
6656   _java_fields_count(0),
6657   _need_verify(false),
6658   _relax_verify(false),
6659   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6660   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6661   _has_final_method(false),
6662   _has_contended_fields(false),
6663   _has_inline_type_fields(false),
6664   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6665   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6666   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6667   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6668   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6669   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6670   _implements_identityObject(false),
6671   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6672   _has_finalizer(false),
6673   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6674   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6675   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6676 
6677   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6678   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6679 
6680   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6681   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6682   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6683   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6684   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6685   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6686   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6687 
6688   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6689   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6690     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6691     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6692     // for those classes.
6693     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6694                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6695   }
6696   else {
6697     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6698                                                stream->need_verify());
6699   }
6700   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6701     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6702     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6703       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6704         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6705         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6706           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6707           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6708           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6709           // calls patch_class().
6710           //
6711           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6712           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6713           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6714           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6715         }
6716       }
6717     }
6718   }
6719 
6720   // synch back verification state to stream
6721   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6722 
6723   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6724   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6725   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6726 
6727   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6728 
6729   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6730 }
6731 
6732 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6733   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6734   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6735   _cp = NULL;
6736   _fields = NULL;
6737   _methods = NULL;
6738   _inner_classes = NULL;
6739   _nest_members = NULL;
6740   _permitted_subclasses = NULL;
6741   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6742   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6743   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6744   _record_components = NULL;
6745 }
6746 
6747 // Destructor to clean up
6748 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6749   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6750 
6751   if (_cp != NULL) {
6752     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6753   }
6754   if (_fields != NULL) {
6755     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6756   }
6757 
6758   if (_methods != NULL) {
6759     // Free methods
6760     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6761   }
6762 
6763   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6764   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6765     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6766   }
6767 
6768   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6769     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6770   }
6771 
6772   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6773     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6774   }
6775 
6776   if (_permitted_subclasses != NULL && _permitted_subclasses != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6777     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _permitted_subclasses);
6778   }
6779 
6780   // Free interfaces
6781   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6782                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6783 
6784   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6785     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6786     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6787 
6788     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6789     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6790 
6791     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6792     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6793     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6794     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6795     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6796     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6797   } else {
6798     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6799     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6800     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6801     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6802     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6803     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6804   }
6805 
6806   clear_class_metadata();
6807   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6808   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6809 
6810   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6811   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6812   // at a safepoint.
6813   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6814     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6815   }
6816 }
6817 
6818 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6819                                    TRAPS) {
6820 
6821   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6822   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6823 
6824   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6825   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6826   // Magic value
6827   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6828   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6829                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6830                      magic, CHECK);
6831 
6832   // Version numbers
6833   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6834   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6835 
6836   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6837     ResourceMark rm;
6838     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6839             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6840     Exceptions::fthrow(
6841       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6842       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6843       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6844       _major_version,
6845       _minor_version);
6846   }
6847 
6848   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6849   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6850 
6851   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6852   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6853 
6854   guarantee_property(
6855     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6856     cp_size, CHECK);
6857 
6858   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6859   if (is_hidden()) { // Add a slot for hidden class name.
6860     assert(_max_num_patched_klasses == 0, "Sanity check");
6861     cp_size++;
6862   } else {
6863     if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6864       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6865     }
6866     cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6867   }
6868 
6869   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6870                                cp_size,
6871                                CHECK);
6872 
6873   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6874 
6875   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6876 
6877   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6878 
6879   // ACCESS FLAGS
6880   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6881 
6882   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6883   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6884   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6885     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6886   }
6887   // JVM_ACC_INLINE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6888   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6889     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_INLINE;
6890   }
6891 
6892   // Access flags
6893   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6894 
6895   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6896     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6897     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6898   }
6899 
6900   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6901 
6902   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6903   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6904     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6905     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6906     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6907   }
6908 
6909   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6910 
6911   // This class and superclass
6912   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6913   check_property(
6914     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6915       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6916     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6917     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6918 
6919   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6920   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6921 
6922   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6923   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6924   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6925   if (_need_verify) {
6926     guarantee_property(class_name_in_cp->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6927                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6928                        CHECK);
6929   }
6930 
6931 #ifdef ASSERT
6932   // Basic sanity checks
6933   assert(!(_is_hidden && (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL)), "mutually exclusive variants");
6934 
6935   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6936     assert(_class_name == vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "A named anonymous class???");
6937   }
6938   if (_is_hidden) {
6939     assert(_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "hidden classes should have a special name");
6940   }
6941 #endif
6942 
6943   // Update the _class_name as needed depending on whether this is a named,
6944   // un-named, hidden or unsafe-anonymous class.
6945 
6946   if (_is_hidden) {
6947     assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6948 #ifdef ASSERT
6949     if (_need_verify) {
6950       verify_legal_class_name(_class_name, CHECK);
6951     }
6952 #endif
6953 
6954   // NOTE: !_is_hidden does not imply "findable" as it could be an old-style
6955   //       "hidden" unsafe-anonymous class
6956 
6957   // If this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it is in the unnamed
6958   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6959   // its host class.
6960   } else if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6961     update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6962     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6963 
6964   } else {
6965     // Check if name in class file matches given name
6966     if (_class_name != class_name_in_cp) {
6967       if (_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name()) {
6968         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6969         Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6970                            vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6971                            "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6972                            class_name_in_cp->as_C_string(),
6973                            _class_name->as_C_string()
6974                            );
6975         return;
6976       } else {
6977         // The class name was not known by the caller so we set it from
6978         // the value in the CP.
6979         update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6980       }
6981       // else nothing to do: the expected class name matches what is in the CP
6982     }
6983   }
6984 
6985   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6986   // asserts that that's the case.
6987   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6988 
6989   if (!is_internal()) {
6990     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6991     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6992       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6993       LogStream ls(lt);
6994       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6995       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6996         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6997       }
6998       ls.cr();
6999     }
7000 
7001 #if INCLUDE_CDS
7002     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
7003       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
7004         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
7005         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
7006       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
7007                  !_is_hidden &&
7008                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
7009         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
7010         // Hidden and unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
7011         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
7012         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7013         bool skip = false;
7014         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
7015           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
7016           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
7017           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
7018           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
7019             skip = true;
7020           }
7021 
7022           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
7023             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
7024             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
7025             skip = false;
7026           }
7027         }
7028         if (skip) {
7029           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
7030             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
7031         } else {
7032           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
7033           classlist_file->flush();
7034         }
7035       }
7036     }
7037 #endif
7038   }
7039 
7040   // SUPERKLASS
7041   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
7042   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
7043                                    _super_class_index,
7044                                    _need_verify,
7045                                    CHECK);
7046 
7047   // Interfaces
7048   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
7049   parse_interfaces(stream,
7050                    _itfs_len,
7051                    cp,
7052                    is_inline_type(),
7053                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
7054                    &_is_declared_atomic,
7055                    CHECK);
7056 
7057   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7058 
7059   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
7060   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
7061   parse_fields(stream,
7062                is_interface(),
7063                is_inline_type(),
7064                _fac,
7065                cp,
7066                cp_size,
7067                &_java_fields_count,
7068                CHECK);
7069 
7070   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
7071 
7072   // Methods
7073   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
7074   parse_methods(stream,
7075                 is_interface(),
7076                 is_inline_type(),
7077                 &promoted_flags,
7078                 &_has_final_method,
7079                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
7080                 CHECK);
7081 
7082   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
7083 
7084   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
7085   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
7086 
7087   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
7088     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7089   }
7090 
7091   // Additional attributes/annotations
7092   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
7093   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
7094 
7095   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
7096 
7097   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
7098   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
7099   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
7100 
7101   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
7102   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
7103                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
7104                      CHECK);
7105 
7106   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
7107 }
7108 
7109 void ClassFileParser::mangle_hidden_class_name(InstanceKlass* const ik) {
7110   ResourceMark rm;
7111   // Construct hidden name from _class_name, "+", and &ik. Note that we can't
7112   // use a '/' because that confuses finding the class's package.  Also, can't
7113   // use an illegal char such as ';' because that causes serialization issues
7114   // and issues with hidden classes that create their own hidden classes.
7115   char addr_buf[20];
7116   jio_snprintf(addr_buf, 20, INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(ik));
7117   size_t new_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length() + 2 + strlen(addr_buf);
7118   char* new_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, new_name_len);
7119   jio_snprintf(new_name, new_name_len, "%s+%s",
7120                _class_name->as_C_string(), addr_buf);
7121   update_class_name(SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_name));
7122 
7123   // Add a Utf8 entry containing the hidden name.
7124   assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
7125   int hidden_index = _orig_cp_size; // this is an extra slot we added
7126   _cp->symbol_at_put(hidden_index, _class_name);
7127 
7128   // Update this_class_index's slot in the constant pool with the new Utf8 entry.
7129   // We have to update the resolved_klass_index and the name_index together
7130   // so extract the existing resolved_klass_index first.
7131   CPKlassSlot cp_klass_slot = _cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index);
7132   int resolved_klass_index = cp_klass_slot.resolved_klass_index();
7133   _cp->unresolved_klass_at_put(_this_class_index, hidden_index, resolved_klass_index);
7134   assert(_cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index).name_index() == _orig_cp_size,
7135          "Bad name_index");
7136 }
7137 
7138 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
7139                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
7140                                                  TRAPS) {
7141   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
7142   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
7143   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
7144   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
7145 
7146   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
7147     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
7148         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
7149         CHECK);
7150   }
7151   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
7152   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
7153     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
7154     if (is_interface()) {
7155       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
7156       // errors not checked yet.
7157       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
7158         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
7159         CHECK);
7160     }
7161     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7162     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
7163                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
7164                                                                super_class_name,
7165                                                                loader,
7166                                                                _protection_domain,
7167                                                                true,
7168                                                                CHECK);
7169   }
7170 
7171   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
7172     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
7173       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7174     }
7175     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
7176       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7177     }
7178 
7179     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
7180       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7181       Exceptions::fthrow(
7182         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7183         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7184         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7185         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7186         _super_klass->external_name()
7187       );
7188       return;
7189     }
7190 
7191     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7192     // are acceptable super classes.
7193     if (is_inline_type()) {
7194       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7195       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7196         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7197         Exceptions::fthrow(
7198           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7199           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7200           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7201           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7202           _super_klass->external_name());
7203         return;
7204       }
7205     }
7206   }
7207 
7208   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7209     // This is the original source of this condition.
7210     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7211     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7212   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7213     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7214     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7215     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7216       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7217     }
7218   }
7219 
7220   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7221   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7222   // returns true
7223   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7224       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7225       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7226     set_invalid_inline_super();
7227   }
7228 
7229   if (!is_inline_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7230       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7231     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7232     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7233   }
7234   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7235   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7236     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7237   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7238     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7239   } else {
7240     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7241     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7242       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7243     }
7244   }
7245   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7246   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7247 
7248   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7249   _transitive_interfaces =
7250     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7251                                   _local_interfaces,
7252                                   _loader_data,
7253                                   CHECK);
7254 
7255   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7256 
7257   // sort methods
7258   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7259 
7260   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7261 
7262   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7263   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7264                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7265                                                     _all_mirandas,
7266                                                     _super_klass,
7267                                                     _methods,
7268                                                     _access_flags,
7269                                                     _major_version,
7270                                                     loader,
7271                                                     _class_name,
7272                                                     _local_interfaces,
7273                                                     CHECK);
7274 
7275   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7276   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7277     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7278 
7279   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7280   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7281 
7282 
7283   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7284     if (Signature::basic_type(fs.signature()) == T_INLINE_TYPE  && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7285       // Pre-load inline class
7286       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_type_field_or_fail(&fs,
7287           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7288           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7289       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7290       assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Value type expected");
7291     }
7292   }
7293 
7294   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7295   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7296     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7297         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_inline_type(),
7298         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7299     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7300     if (is_inline_type()) {
7301       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7302       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7303       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7304     }
7305   } else {
7306     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7307   }
7308   _has_inline_type_fields = _field_info->_has_inline_fields;
7309 
7310   // Compute reference type
7311   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7312 }
7313 
7314 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7315 
7316 #ifdef ASSERT
7317   if (klass != NULL) {
7318     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7319   }
7320 #endif
7321 
7322   _klass = klass;
7323 }
7324 
7325 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7326 
7327 #ifdef ASSERT
7328   if (klass != NULL) {
7329     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7330   }
7331 #endif
7332 
7333   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7334 }
7335 
7336 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7337 // clone stream with rewound position
7338 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7339   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7340 
7341   return _stream->clone();
7342 }

7344 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7345 // debugging
7346 
7347 #ifdef ASSERT
7348 
7349 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7350 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7351   if (class_name != NULL) {
7352     ResourceMark rm;
7353     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7354     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7355   } else {
7356     return true;
7357   }
7358 }

7360 #endif
